Tool reply2026-05-26T22:55:34.913Z
1	# 4M Training on THINGS (Vision + MEG/EEG)
2	
3	Train [4M](https://github.com/apple/ml-4m) on pretokenized THINGS shards with RGB, depth, MEG, and EEG — without modifying `external/ml-4m/`.
4	
5	Volume layout: [`modal/data/README.md`](../modal/data/README.md).
6	
7	## Quickstart
8	
9	```bash
10	python 4m_training/train_4m.py demo
11	python 4m_training/train_4m.py validate --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
12	python 4m_training/train_4m.py dryrun --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
13	python 4m_training/train_4m.py train --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
14	modal run 4m_training/modal_train.py --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
15	pytest 4m_training/ -v
16	```
17	
18	## Files (every file justified)
19	
20	| File | Why it exists |
21	|------|----------------|
22	| **`train_4m.py`** | Entry point: demo / dryrun / delegates to `run_training_4m.py` |
23	| **`fourm_neural_modalities.py`** | Registers `tok_meg`, `tok_eeg`, masks into stock `MODALITY_INFO` |
24	| **`fourm_neural_transforms.py`** | Stock `AbstractTransform` adapters (trial pick in `preprocess`) |
25	| **`neural_trial_transform.py`** | Collapse `(n_trials, …)` shards → flat token seq; sentinel handling |
26	| **`neural_masking.py`** | Subclass of stock `UnifiedMasking`; zero budget when mask=0 |
27	| **`things_augmenter.py`** | Subclass of stock `PreTokenizedImageAugmenter`; no `crop_settings` tars |
28	| **`fourm_dataloader.py`** | Patches above into stock 4M + small WDS val loader (stock val is folder-only) |
29	| **`modal_train.py`** | Modal GPU wrapper around `train_4m.py train` |
30	| **`configs/4m_things_main.yaml`** | Model, optimizer, token budgets, paths |
31	| **`configs/4m_things_data.yaml`** | Train/val `data_path`, domains, Dirichlet alphas |
32	| **`test_*.py`** | Contract tests: shard layout, stock decode, trial/masking logic, loader integration |
33	
34	Train uses stock `get_train_dataloader` → `build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader`. Custom code is limited to modality registration, three small patches, and val-on-tars.
35	
36	## Config
37	
38	Production layout (what downstream users should copy):
39	
40	- **`configs/4m_things_main.yaml`** — model, optimizer, `data_config:` pointer, `output_dir` on the volume
41	- **`configs/4m_things_data.yaml`** — `train` / `val` datasets, `data_path` under `/project/data/...`
42	
43	All training data lives on the shared Modal **`project`** volume; you do not need separate repo directories per dataset. Point `data_path` at `/project/data/train/things/...` or `/project/data/train/cc12m/...`.
44	
45	Edit **`4m_things_data.yaml`** for `in_domains` / `out_domains` / alphas. Keep `meg_mask` / `eeg_mask` out of domain lists (presence flags only). To try a new task without touching the main config, swap only the data file:
46	
47	```bash
48	python 4m_training/train_4m.py train --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml -- \
49	  --data_config 4m_training/configs/4m_smoke_things_rgb2meg_data.yaml
50	```
51	
52	### Modal: avoid rebuilding the image every time
53	
54	The Modal image only caches **pip/apt** deps (`4m_training/modal_image.py`). Your repo is **mounted at container start**, not copied into the image, so editing YAML or Python does not trigger a multi-minute torch reinstall.
55	
56	**Fast iteration (no GPU train):**
57	
58	```bash
59	pytest 4m_training/ -v                                   # configs + synthetic shards
60	python 4m_training/train_4m.py validate --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
61	modal run 4m_training/modal_train.py --dryrun --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
62	modal run 4m_training/modal_smoke_train.py --case probe   # CPU, checks volume paths
63	```
64	
65	**GPU smoke train** (only after dryrun passes): `modal run 4m_training/modal_smoke_train.py --case prod_things`
66	
67	Rebuild happens only if you change the package list in `modal_image.py` or Modal’s Python version.
68	
69	## Token shapes
70	
71	Defined in `neural_constants.py` (import constants instead of hardcoding literals):
72	
73	| Modality | On-disk | After trial pick | Vocab constant |
74	|----------|---------|------------------|----------------|
75	| `tok_meg` | `(n_trials, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)` | `(MEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,)` | `MEG_VOCAB_SIZE` |
76	| `tok_eeg` | `(n_trials, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)` | `(EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,)` | `EEG_VOCAB_SIZE` |
77	| `tok_rgb` | `(TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,)` int16 | — | `TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE` |
78	
79	Missing neural: sentinel `(1, …)` filled with `-1`, mask `0`.
80

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:01.453Z
1	"""Train 4M on THINGS with vision + MEG/EEG neural modalities.
2	
3	Thin wrapper around 4M's ``run_training_4m.py``. Neural modalities and
4	dataloaders are registered/patched at import time — no ``external/ml-4m/`` edits.
5	
6	Modes::
7	
8	    python 4m_training/train_4m.py demo
9	    python 4m_training/train_4m.py dryrun --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_data.yaml
10	    python 4m_training/train_4m.py train --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
11	    python 4m_training/train_4m.py validate --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
12	"""
13	
14	from __future__ import annotations
15	
16	import argparse
17	import io
18	import sys
19	import tarfile
20	import tempfile
21	from functools import partial
22	from pathlib import Path
23	from typing import Any
24	
25	import numpy as np
26	
27	_HERE = Path(__file__).resolve().parent
28	_REPO_ROOT = _HERE.parent
29	sys.path.insert(0, str(_HERE))
30	
31	import fourm_neural_modalities  # noqa: F401,E402
32	from fourm_dataloader import patch_pretrain_utils
33	from neural_constants import (
34	    EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
35	    MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
36	    THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
37	    THINGS_PATCH_SIZE,
38	    TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,
39	    pretoken_grid_num_tokens,
40	)
41	
42	patch_pretrain_utils()
43	
44	
45	def _make_tar(path: Path, entries: list[tuple[str, str, bytes]]) -> None:
46	    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
47	    with tarfile.open(path, "w") as tar:
48	        for key, ext, data in entries:
49	            info = tarfile.TarInfo(name=f"{key}.{ext}")
50	            info.size = len(data)
51	            tar.addfile(info, io.BytesIO(data))
52	
53	
54	def _npy_bytes(arr: np.ndarray) -> bytes:
55	    buf = io.BytesIO()
56	    np.save(buf, arr, allow_pickle=False)
57	    return buf.getvalue()
58	
59	
60	def run_demo() -> None:
61	    """Build a synthetic shard and walk samples through the 4M decode path."""
62	    import webdataset as wds
63	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import (
64	        filter_metadata,
65	        multi_tarfile_samples,
66	        remove_extensions,
67	        tok_to_int64,
68	        wds_decoder,
69	    )
70	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import map as keyless_map
71	
72	    from fourm_neural_transforms import EegTokTransform, MegTokTransform
73	
74	    with tempfile.TemporaryDirectory() as tmp:
75	        root = Path(tmp) / "things"
76	        ids = ["000000001", "000000002", "000000003"]
77	
78	        rgb_arr = lambda i: np.full((TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,), int(i), dtype=np.int16)
79	        depth_arr = np.zeros((TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE,), dtype=np.int16)
80	        meg_real = np.full((4, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), 7, dtype=np.int16)
81	        meg_sentinel = np.full((1, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
82	        eeg_real = np.full((2, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), 3, dtype=np.int16)
83	        eeg_sentinel = np.full((1, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE), -1, dtype=np.int16)
84	        mask_real = np.array([1], dtype=np.uint8)
85	        mask_zero = np.array([0], dtype=np.uint8)
86	
87	        for mod, arrs in [
88	            ("tok_rgb", [(i, _npy_bytes(rgb_arr(i))) for i in ids]),
89	            ("tok_depth", [(i, _npy_bytes(depth_arr)) for i in ids]),
90	            (
91	                "tok_meg",
92	                [
93	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(meg_real)),
94	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(meg_sentinel)),
95	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(meg_real)),
96	                ],
97	            ),
98	            (
99	                "tok_eeg",
100	                [
101	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(eeg_real)),
102	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(eeg_sentinel)),
103	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(eeg_real)),
104	                ],
105	            ),
106	            (
107	                "meg_mask",
108	                [
109	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
110	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(mask_zero)),
111	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
112	                ],
113	            ),
114	            (
115	                "eeg_mask",
116	                [
117	                    ("000000001", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
118	                    ("000000002", _npy_bytes(mask_zero)),
119	                    ("000000003", _npy_bytes(mask_real)),
120	                ],
121	            ),
122	        ]:
123	            _make_tar(
124	                root / f"{mod}/shard_000.tar",
125	                [(k, "npy", b) for k, b in arrs],
126	            )
127	
128	        url = (
129	            f"{root}/[tok_rgb,tok_depth,tok_meg,tok_eeg,meg_mask,eeg_mask]/"
130	            "shard_000.tar"
131	        )
132	        print(f"data_path = {url}\n")
133	
134	        pipeline = wds.DataPipeline(
135	            wds.SimpleShardList(url),
136	            partial(multi_tarfile_samples, handler=lambda e: (_ for _ in ()).throw(e)),
137	            wds.decode(wds_decoder),
138	            wds.map(remove_extensions),
139	            keyless_map(filter_metadata),
140	            keyless_map(tok_to_int64),
141	        )
142	
143	        print("=" * 72)
144	        print("  4M pipeline output (after decode + filter)")
145	        print("=" * 72)
146	        for sample in pipeline:
147	            shapes = {
148	                k: getattr(v, "shape", type(v).__name__) for k, v in sample.items()
149	            }
150	            print(f"  modalities = {sorted(sample)}")
151	            print(f"  shapes     = {shapes}")
152	            print()
153	
154	        print("=" * 72)
155	        print("  After trial transforms")
156	        print("=" * 72)
157	        meg_tx = MegTokTransform(training=True, seed=0)
158	        eeg_tx = EegTokTransform(training=True, seed=0)
159	        for label, arr, tx in [
160	            ("MEG real", meg_real, meg_tx),
161	            ("MEG sentinel", meg_sentinel, meg_tx),
162	            ("EEG real", eeg_real, eeg_tx),
163	            ("EEG sentinel", eeg_sentinel, eeg_tx),
164	        ]:
165	            tokens = tx.preprocess(arr)
166	            print(f"  {label:>14s}: in={tuple(arr.shape)} -> out={tuple(tokens.shape)}")
167	
168	
169	def _load_configs(config_path: Path) -> tuple[dict[str, Any], dict[str, Any], dict[str, Any]]:
170	    """Return (main_cfg, train_ds_cfg, val_ds_cfg_or_empty). Accepts main or data yaml."""
171	    import yaml
172	
173	    config_path = config_path.resolve()
174	    if not config_path.is_absolute():
175	        config_path = (_REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
176	
177	    with open(config_path) as f:
178	        cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
179	
180	    if "train" in cfg and "datasets" in cfg.get("train", {}):
181	        main = {
182	            "input_size": THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
183	            "num_input_tokens": 256,
184	            "num_target_tokens": 256,
185	            "batch_size": 4,
186	            "epoch_size": 64,
187	            "text_tokenizer_path": str(
188	                _REPO_ROOT
189	                / "external/ml-4m/fourm/utils/tokenizer/trained/text_tokenizer_4m_wordpiece_30k.json"
190	            ),
191	        }
192	        train_ds = next(iter(cfg["train"]["datasets"].values()))
193	        val_ds = {}
194	        if "val" in cfg and cfg["val"].get("datasets"):
195	            val_ds = next(iter(cfg["val"]["datasets"].values()))
196	        return main, train_ds, val_ds
197	
198	    data_rel = cfg.get("data_config")
199	    if not data_rel:
200	        raise ValueError(f"{config_path}: expected data_config or train.datasets")
201	    data_path = Path(data_rel)
202	    if not data_path.is_absolute():
203	        data_path = (_REPO_ROOT / data_path).resolve()
204	    with open(data_path) as f:
205	        data_cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
206	    train_ds = next(iter(data_cfg["train"]["datasets"].values()))
207	    val_ds = {}
208	    if "val" in data_cfg and data_cfg["val"].get("datasets"):
209	        val_ds = next(iter(data_cfg["val"]["datasets"].values()))
210	    return cfg, train_ds, val_ds
211

213	def run_validate(config_path: Path) -> None:
214	    from config_validate import validate_config_file
215	
216	    errors = validate_config_file(config_path, _REPO_ROOT)
217	    if errors:
218	        print(f"FAIL {config_path}:")
219	        for e in errors:
220	            print(f"  - {e}")
221	        raise SystemExit(1)
222	    print(f"OK {config_path}")

225	def _build_modality_info(
226	    all_domain_names: list[str],
227	    input_size: int = THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE,
228	) -> dict:
229	    import copy
230	
231	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
232	
233	    # Model + masking only need in/out token domains, not presence flags.
234	    token_domains = [d for d in all_domain_names if not d.endswith("_mask")]
235	    modality_info = {
236	        mod: copy.deepcopy(MODALITY_INFO[mod])
237	        for mod in token_domains
238	        if mod in MODALITY_INFO
239	    }
240	    for mod, info in modality_info.items():
241	        if info.get("type") == "img":
242	            patch_size = info.get("patch_size", THINGS_PATCH_SIZE)
243	            info["max_tokens"] = pretoken_grid_num_tokens(input_size, patch_size)
244	    return modality_info
245	
246	
247	def _iterate_loader(loader, n_batches: int, label: str) -> None:
248	    print(f"{label}: iterating {n_batches} batches…\n")
249	    for i, batch in enumerate(loader):
250	        if i >= n_batches:
251	            break
252	        print(f"batch {i}: keys = {sorted(batch.keys())}")
253	        for k, v in batch.items():
254	            if isinstance(v, dict) and "tensor" in v:
255	                print(f"  {k:>16s} : tensor shape={tuple(v['tensor'].shape)}")
256	            else:
257	                shape = getattr(v, "shape", None)
258	                print(
259	                    f"  {k:>16s} : shape={tuple(shape) if shape is not None else type(v).__name__}"
260	                )
261	        print()
262	
263	
264	def run_dryrun(config_path: Path, n_batches: int = 4) -> None:
265	    """Build train + val dataloaders and iterate a few batches."""
266	    from tokenizers import Tokenizer
267	
268	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
269	    from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import get_train_dataloader, get_val_dataloader, setup_sampling_mod_info
270	
271	    main_cfg, train_ds, val_ds = _load_configs(config_path)
272	    input_size = main_cfg.get("input_size", THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE)
273	
274	    in_domains = sorted(train_ds["in_domains"].split("-"))
275	    out_domains = sorted(train_ds["out_domains"].split("-"))
276	    all_domains = sorted(set(in_domains) | set(out_domains))
277	    modality_info_full = _build_modality_info(all_domains, input_size)
278	    mod_info, sampling_weights = setup_sampling_mod_info(train_ds, modality_info_full)
279	
280	    tok_path = main_cfg.get(
281	        "text_tokenizer_path",
282	        str(_REPO_ROOT / "external/ml-4m/fourm/utils/tokenizer/trained/text_tokenizer_4m_wordpiece_30k.json"),
283	    )
284	    text_tokenizer = Tokenizer.from_file(tok_path)
285	
286	    train_loader = get_train_dataloader(
287	        dataset_config=train_ds,
288	        modality_info=mod_info,
289	        sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
290	        text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
291	        input_size=input_size,
292	        num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
293	        num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
294	        min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
295	        min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
296	        num_tasks=1,
297	        num_workers=0,
298	        dataset_batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
299	        epoch_size=main_cfg.get("epoch_size", max(n_batches * 4, 16)),
300	    )
301	    _iterate_loader(train_loader, n_batches, "train dryrun")
302	
303	    if val_ds.get("data_path"):
304	        val_loader = get_val_dataloader(
305	            dataset_config=val_ds,
306	            dataset_name="things",
307	            train_configs={"things": train_ds},
308	            modality_info=mod_info,
309	            sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
310	            text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
311	            input_size=input_size,
312	            num_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_input_tokens", 128),
313	            num_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("num_target_tokens", 128),
314	            min_input_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_input_tokens"),
315	            min_target_tokens=main_cfg.get("min_target_tokens"),
316	            fixed_eval=False,
317	            fixed_eval_input_tokens=128,
318	            fixed_eval_target_tokens=128,
319	            dist_eval=False,
320	            num_tasks=1,
321	            num_workers=0,
322	            batch_size=main_cfg.get("batch_size", 4),
323	            pin_mem=False,
324	        )
325	        _iterate_loader(val_loader, n_batches, "val dryrun")
326	
327	
328	def run_train(config_path: Path, extra_argv: list[str]) -> None:
329	    """Hand off to 4M's official trainer with neural patches active."""
330	    import os
331	    import runpy
332	
333	    # Stock run_training_4m.py always uses DDP; set single-process vars if missing.
334	    os.environ.setdefault("RANK", "0")
335	    os.environ.setdefault("WORLD_SIZE", "1")
336	    os.environ.setdefault("LOCAL_RANK", "0")
337	    os.environ.setdefault("MASTER_ADDR", "127.0.0.1")
338	    os.environ.setdefault("MASTER_PORT", "29500")
339	
340	    ml_4m_root = _REPO_ROOT / "external" / "ml-4m"
341	    if not (ml_4m_root / "run_training_4m.py").exists():
342	        raise FileNotFoundError(
343	            f"4M trainer not found at {ml_4m_root}. "
344	            "Install with: pip install -e external/ml-4m"
345	        )
346	    sys.path.insert(0, str(ml_4m_root))
347	    config_path = config_path.resolve()
348	    if not config_path.is_absolute():
349	        config_path = (_REPO_ROOT / config_path).resolve()
350	
351	    sys.argv = ["run_training_4m.py", "-c", str(config_path), *extra_argv]
352	    print(f"handing off to 4M trainer: argv = {sys.argv}\n")
353	    runpy.run_path(str(ml_4m_root / "run_training_4m.py"), run_name="__main__")
354	
355	
356	def main() -> None:
357	    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
358	        description=__doc__,
359	        formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,
360	    )
361	    sub = p.add_subparsers(dest="mode", required=True)
362	
363	    sub.add_parser("demo", help="Synthetic shard pipeline walkthrough.")
364	
365	    p_dry = sub.add_parser("dryrun", help="Iterate train + val batches from config.")
366	    p_dry.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
367	    p_dry.add_argument("--n-batches", type=int, default=4)
368	
369	    p_train = sub.add_parser("train", help="Run 4M run_training_4m.py.")
370	    p_train.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
371	    p_train.add_argument("extra", nargs=argparse.REMAINDER)
372	
373	    p_val = sub.add_parser("validate", help="Check main/data YAML against 4M (no GPU/data).")
374	    p_val.add_argument("--config", type=Path, required=True)
375	
376	    args = p.parse_args()
377	    if args.mode == "demo":
378	        run_demo()
379	    elif args.mode == "dryrun":
380	        run_dryrun(args.config, args.n_batches)
381	    elif args.mode == "validate":
382	        run_validate(args.config)
383	    elif args.mode == "train":
384	        run_train(args.config, args.extra or [])
385	
386	
387	if __name__ == "__main__":
388	    main()

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:04.312Z
1	"""Minimal hooks so stock 4M dataloaders work with THINGS neural shards.
2	
3	We do **not** reimplement the WebDataset pipeline. Instead we patch three
4	integration points and delegate everything else to upstream 4M:
5	
6	  * ``UnifiedMasking`` → ``PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking`` (meg/eeg absence)
7	  * ``PreTokenizedImageAugmenter`` → ``ThingsImageAugmenter`` (optional crop_settings)
8	  * ``get_val_dataloader`` → WDS branch when ``use_wds: true`` (stock val is folder-only)
9	
10	Train uses stock ``get_train_dataloader`` → ``build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader`` unchanged.
11	Neural transforms are stock ``AbstractTransform`` subclasses registered in
12	``MODALITY_TRANSFORMS`` via ``fourm_neural_modalities``.
13	"""
14	
15	from __future__ import annotations
16	
17	import copy
18	from functools import partial
19	
20	import webdataset as wds
21	from fourm.data import pretrain_utils
22	from fourm.data import unified_datasets as ud
23	from fourm.data import image_augmenter as ia
24	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import CropSettingsTransform, IdentityTransform
25	from fourm.data.pretrain_utils import cfgs_get
26	from fourm.data.unified_datasets import (
27	    default_collate,
28	    filter_metadata,
29	    map,
30	    multi_tarfile_samples,
31	    remove_extensions,
32	    rename_modalities,
33	    tok_to_int64,
34	    wds_decoder,
35	)
36	import torchvision.transforms as transforms
37	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import UnifiedDataTransform
38	
39	import fourm_neural_modalities
40	from neural_masking import PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
41	from things_augmenter import ThingsImageAugmenter
42	
43	_PRESENCE_PATHS = {"meg_mask": "meg_mask", "eeg_mask": "eeg_mask"}
44	
45	_ORIG_UNIFIED_MASKING = ud.UnifiedMasking
46	_ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG = ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter
47	_ORIG_GET_VAL = pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader
48	_ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES = ud.rename_modalities
49	_PATCHED = False
50

52	def _rename_modalities(sample, modality_paths):
53	    """Stock rename assumes every path exists; THINGS omits optional ``crop_settings`` tars."""
54	    present = {out: src for out, src in modality_paths.items() if src in sample}
55	    if not present:
56	        return sample
57	    return _ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES(sample, present)
58	
59	
60	def _extend_modality_paths(modality_info: dict) -> dict[str, str]:
61	    paths = {mod: modality_info[mod].get("path", None) or mod for mod in modality_info}
62	    paths.update(_PRESENCE_PATHS)
63	    return paths
64	
65	
66	def _wds_eval_loader(
67	    data_path: str,
68	    all_domains: list[str],
69	    modality_info: dict,
70	    modality_transforms: dict,
71	    image_augmenter,
72	    text_tokenizer,
73	    input_tokens_range,
74	    target_tokens_range,
75	    num_workers: int,
76	    batch_size: int,
77	    sampling_weights=None,
78	    modality_name_map=None,
79	):
80	    """Deterministic WDS val loader — only gap stock 4M does not cover.
81	
82	    Reuses the same transform stack as ``build_wds_fm_pretraining_dataloader``
83	    (``UnifiedDataTransform`` + patched ``PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking``).
84	    Pipeline differs only in shard source (``SimpleShardList``, no shuffle/repeat).
85	    """
86	    fourm_neural_modalities.register(training=False)
87	
88	    modality_paths = _extend_modality_paths(modality_info)
89	    modality_transforms = copy.deepcopy(modality_transforms)
90	    if any(modality_info[d].get("pretokenized", False) for d in all_domains):
91	        modality_transforms["crop_settings"] = CropSettingsTransform()
92	    modality_transforms["__key__"] = IdentityTransform()
93	
94	    transform = transforms.Compose(
95	        [
96	            UnifiedDataTransform(
97	                transforms_dict=modality_transforms,
98	                image_augmenter=image_augmenter,
99	            ),
100	            PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(
101	                modality_info=modality_info,
102	                text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
103	                input_tokens_range=input_tokens_range,
104	                target_tokens_range=target_tokens_range,
105	                sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
106	            ),
107	        ]
108	    )
109	
110	    datapipe = wds.DataPipeline(
111	        wds.SimpleShardList(data_path),
112	        partial(multi_tarfile_samples, modality_name_map=modality_name_map),
113	        wds.decode(wds_decoder),
114	        wds.map(remove_extensions),
115	        map(filter_metadata),
116	        map(tok_to_int64),
117	        map(partial(rename_modalities, modality_paths=modality_paths)),
118	        map(transform),
119	        wds.batched(batch_size, collation_fn=default_collate, partial=False),
120	    )
121	    return wds.WebLoader(datapipe, num_workers=num_workers, batch_size=None)
122	
123	
124	def _neural_get_val_dataloader(
125	    dataset_config,
126	    dataset_name,
127	    train_configs,
128	    modality_info,
129	    sampling_weights,
130	    text_tokenizer,
131	    input_size,
132	    num_input_tokens,
133	    num_target_tokens,
134	    min_input_tokens,
135	    min_target_tokens,
136	    fixed_eval,
137	    fixed_eval_input_tokens,
138	    fixed_eval_target_tokens,
139	    dist_eval,
140	    num_tasks,
141	    num_workers,
142	    batch_size,
143	    pin_mem,
144	):
145	    """Stock val loader, plus WDS tars when ``use_wds: true`` in val config."""
146	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
147	    from fourm.data.modality_transforms import CaptionTransform
148	    from fourm.data.image_augmenter import CenterCropImageAugmenter
149	
150	    dataset_type = cfgs_get("type", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs)
151	    use_wds = cfgs_get("use_wds", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs, False)
152	
153	    if not (dataset_type == "multimodal" and use_wds):
154	        return _ORIG_GET_VAL(
155	            dataset_config,
156	            dataset_name,
157	            train_configs,
158	            modality_info,
159	            sampling_weights,
160	            text_tokenizer,
161	            input_size,
162	            num_input_tokens,
163	            num_target_tokens,
164	            min_input_tokens,
165	            min_target_tokens,
166	            fixed_eval,
167	            fixed_eval_input_tokens,
168	            fixed_eval_target_tokens,
169	            dist_eval,
170	            num_tasks,
171	            num_workers,
172	            batch_size,
173	            pin_mem,
174	        )
175	
176	    in_domains = sorted(
177	        cfgs_get("in_domains", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs).split("-")
178	    )
179	    out_domains = sorted(
180	        cfgs_get("out_domains", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs).split("-")
181	    )
182	    all_domains = sorted(set(in_domains) | set(out_domains))
183	
184	    modality_transforms = MODALITY_TRANSFORMS
185	    if "caption" in modality_transforms:
186	        modality_transforms["caption"] = CaptionTransform(
187	            aligned_captions=cfgs_get(
188	                "aligned_captions", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs, True
189	            )
190	        )
191	
192	    main_augment_domain = cfgs_get(
193	        "main_augment_domain", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs
194	    )
195	    is_pretokenized = any(
196	        modality_info[mod].get("pretokenized", False) for mod in modality_info
197	    )
198	    eval_image_augmenter = (
199	        ThingsImageAugmenter(
200	            target_size=input_size, no_aug=True, main_domain=main_augment_domain
201	        )
202	        if is_pretokenized
203	        else CenterCropImageAugmenter(
204	            target_size=input_size, main_domain=main_augment_domain
205	        )
206	    )
207	
208	    if fixed_eval:
209	        input_tokens_range = (fixed_eval_input_tokens, fixed_eval_input_tokens)
210	        target_tokens_range = (fixed_eval_target_tokens, fixed_eval_target_tokens)
211	    else:
212	        num_input_tokens = dataset_config.get("num_input_tokens", num_input_tokens)
213	        num_target_tokens = dataset_config.get("num_target_tokens", num_target_tokens)
214	        min_input_tokens = dataset_config.get("min_input_tokens", min_input_tokens)
215	        min_target_tokens = dataset_config.get("min_target_tokens", min_target_tokens)
216	        min_input_tokens = (
217	            num_input_tokens if min_input_tokens is None else min_input_tokens
218	        )
219	        min_target_tokens = (
220	            num_target_tokens if min_target_tokens is None else min_target_tokens
221	        )
222	        input_tokens_range = (min_input_tokens, num_input_tokens)
223	        target_tokens_range = (min_target_tokens, num_target_tokens)
224	
225	    print(
226	        "Warning: Eval stats may vary slightly as the masking applied on images is random."
227	    )
228	    return _wds_eval_loader(
229	        data_path=cfgs_get("data_path", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs),
230	        all_domains=all_domains,
231	        modality_info=modality_info,
232	        modality_transforms=modality_transforms,
233	        image_augmenter=eval_image_augmenter,
234	        text_tokenizer=text_tokenizer,
235	        input_tokens_range=input_tokens_range,
236	        target_tokens_range=target_tokens_range,
237	        num_workers=num_workers,
238	        batch_size=batch_size,
239	        sampling_weights=sampling_weights,
240	        modality_name_map=cfgs_get(
241	            "modality_name_map", dataset_config, dataset_name, train_configs
242	        ),
243	    )
244

246	def patch_pretrain_utils() -> None:
247	    """Install neural hooks into stock 4M (idempotent)."""
248	    global _PATCHED
249	    if _PATCHED:
250	        return
251	
252	    # Stock WDS + folder datasets instantiate these classes by reference.
253	    ud.UnifiedMasking = PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking
254	    ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = ThingsImageAugmenter
255	    pretrain_utils.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = ThingsImageAugmenter
256	    ud.rename_modalities = _rename_modalities
257	
258	    fourm_neural_modalities.register(training=True)
259	
260	    pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader = _neural_get_val_dataloader
261	    import fourm.data as fd
262	
263	    fd.get_val_dataloader = _neural_get_val_dataloader
264	    _PATCHED = True
265	
266	
267	def unpatch_pretrain_utils() -> None:
268	    """Restore stock 4M (for tests)."""
269	    global _PATCHED
270	    ud.UnifiedMasking = _ORIG_UNIFIED_MASKING
271	    ia.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = _ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG
272	    pretrain_utils.PreTokenizedImageAugmenter = _ORIG_PRETOKENIZED_AUG
273	    ud.rename_modalities = _ORIG_RENAME_MODALITIES
274	    pretrain_utils.get_val_dataloader = _ORIG_GET_VAL
275	    import fourm.data as fd
276	
277	    fd.get_val_dataloader = _ORIG_GET_VAL
278	    _PATCHED = False

1	"""Register neural modalities with 4M at import time.
2	
3	Import this module BEFORE any 4M script that reads MODALITY_INFO or builds
4	a dataloader. Mutates ``MODALITY_INFO`` and ``MODALITY_TRANSFORMS`` in place.
5	"""
6	
7	from __future__ import annotations
8	
9	import copy

91	_REGISTERED_TRAINING: bool | None = None
92	
93	
94	def register(training: bool = True) -> None:
95	    """Inject MEG/EEG modalities into 4M's global registries.
96	
97	    Always updates ``MODALITY_TRANSFORMS`` for tok_meg/tok_eeg so train vs val
98	    trial sampling can be switched by calling ``register(training=False)``.
99	    """
100	    global _REGISTERED_TRAINING
101	
102	    for name, info in _NEURAL_MODALITY_INFO.items():
103	        _mi.MODALITY_INFO.setdefault(name, info)
104	
105	    # THINGS on-disk folders use tok_rgb / tok_depth; stock 4M registers @224 names.
106	    for alias, src in (("tok_rgb", "tok_rgb@224"), ("tok_depth", "tok_depth@224")):
107	        if alias not in _mi.MODALITY_INFO and src in _mi.MODALITY_INFO:
108	            info = copy.deepcopy(_mi.MODALITY_INFO[src])
109	            info["path"] = alias
110	            _mi.MODALITY_INFO[alias] = info
111	
112	    _mi.MODALITY_TRANSFORMS["tok_meg"] = MegTokTransform(training=training)
113	    _mi.MODALITY_TRANSFORMS["tok_eeg"] = EegTokTransform(training=training)
114	    _mi.MODALITY_TRANSFORMS.setdefault("meg_mask", MaskFlagTransform())
115	    _mi.MODALITY_TRANSFORMS.setdefault("eeg_mask", MaskFlagTransform())
116	    _REGISTERED_TRAINING = training
117	
118	
119	register()

1	"""4M-compatible AbstractTransform adapters for neural modalities."""

16	class MegTokTransform(AbstractTransform):
17	    """Pick one MEG trial per call and return a (MEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,) int64 tensor."""
18	
19	    def __init__(self, training: bool = True, seed: int | None = None):
20	        self.sampler = MegTrialSampleTransform(training=training, seed=seed)
21	
22	    def load(self, path: str) -> np.ndarray:
23	        return np.load(path, allow_pickle=False)
24	
25	    def preprocess(self, sample: np.ndarray) -> torch.Tensor:
26	        tokens, _valid = self.sampler(sample)
27	        tokens = np.clip(tokens, 0, MEG_CODE_MAX)
28	        return torch.from_numpy(tokens).long()
29	
30	    def image_augment(
31	        self,
32	        v,
33	        crop_coords,
34	        flip,
35	        orig_size,
36	        target_size,
37	        rand_aug_idx,
38	        resample_mode=None,
39	    ):
40	        return v
41	
42	    def postprocess(self, sample):
43	        return sample
44

59

62	
63	    def postprocess(self, sample):
64	        return sample

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:14.553Z
1	"""Generalized trial-sampling for stacked neural token arrays (MEG / EEG).
2	
3	Each ``tok_meg/<image_id>.npy`` or ``tok_eeg/<image_id>.npy`` stores::
4	
5	    arr.shape == (n_trials, *trial_shape)   # int16
6	
7	For images lacking neural data, the packer writes a sentinel::
8	
9	    np.full((1, *trial_shape), NEURAL_SENTINEL_VALUE, dtype=np.int16)
10	
11	Pure-Python; only depends on numpy.
12	"""
13	
14	from __future__ import annotations
15	
16	import numpy as np
17	
18	from neural_constants import (
19	    EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
20	    EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,
21	    MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE,
22	    MEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,
23	    NEURAL_PLACEHOLDER_CODE,
24	    NEURAL_SENTINEL_VALUE,
25	)
26	
27	# Backward-compatible aliases (prefer neural_constants in new code).
28	SENTINEL_VALUE: int = NEURAL_SENTINEL_VALUE
29	PLACEHOLDER_FILL_VALUE: int = NEURAL_PLACEHOLDER_CODE
30	
31	
32	def is_placeholder(arr: np.ndarray, trial_shape: tuple[int, ...]) -> bool:
33	    """Detect sentinel pattern: shape ``(1, *trial_shape)`` filled with -1."""
34	    expected = (1, *trial_shape)
35	    return bool(
36	        arr.ndim == len(expected)
37	        and tuple(arr.shape) == expected
38	        and (arr == NEURAL_SENTINEL_VALUE).all()
39	    )
40	
41	
42	class NeuralTrialSampleTransform:
43	    """Pick one trial per call and flatten to a 4M-compatible token sequence.
44	
45	    Args:
46	        trial_shape: Inner shape per trial, e.g. ``MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE`` or ``EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE``.
47	        training: If True, sample a uniform random trial; if False, always trial 0.
48	        seed: Optional RNG seed for reproducibility within one transform instance.
49	    """
50	
51	    def __init__(
52	        self,
53	        trial_shape: tuple[int, ...],
54	        training: bool = True,
55	        seed: int | None = None,
56	    ):
57	        self.trial_shape = trial_shape
58	        self.tokens_per_trial = int(np.prod(trial_shape))
59	        self.training = training
60	        self.rng = np.random.default_rng(seed)
61	
62	    def __call__(self, arr: np.ndarray) -> tuple[np.ndarray, bool]:
63	        ndim = 1 + len(self.trial_shape)
64	        if arr.ndim != ndim or tuple(arr.shape[1:]) != self.trial_shape:
65	            raise ValueError(
66	                f"Trial array must have shape (n_trials, {self.trial_shape}); "
67	                f"got {arr.shape}"
68	            )
69	
70	        if is_placeholder(arr, self.trial_shape):
71	            tokens = np.full(
72	                (self.tokens_per_trial,),
73	                NEURAL_PLACEHOLDER_CODE,
74	                dtype=np.int32,
75	            )
76	            return tokens, False
77	
78	        n_trials = arr.shape[0]
79	        idx = int(self.rng.integers(0, n_trials)) if self.training else 0
80	        tokens = arr[idx].astype(np.int32).reshape(-1)
81	        assert tokens.shape == (self.tokens_per_trial,)
82	        np.clip(tokens, 0, None, out=tokens)
83	        return tokens, True
84	
85	
86	class MegTrialSampleTransform(NeuralTrialSampleTransform):
87	    """MEG trial sampler: ``(n_trials, *MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)`` -> ``(MEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,)``."""
88	
89	    def __init__(self, training: bool = True, seed: int | None = None):
90	        super().__init__(trial_shape=MEG_TRIAL_SHAPE, training=training, seed=seed)
91	
92	
93	class EegTrialSampleTransform(NeuralTrialSampleTransform):
94	    """EEG trial sampler: ``(n_trials, *EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE)`` -> ``(EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL,)``."""
95	
96	    def __init__(self, training: bool = True, seed: int | None = None):
97	        super().__init__(trial_shape=EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE, training=training, seed=seed)
98

1	"""Single source of truth for THINGS + neural modality geometry and vocab sizes.
2	
3	Import from here instead of scattering literals (512, 8192, 196, 224, …) across
4	transforms, masking, tests, and demos. Values match stock 4M ``tok_*@224`` entries
5	and the BrainOmni / LaBraM tokenizers documented in ``modal/data/README.md``.
6	"""

9	
10	# --- MEG (BrainOmni V512 RVQ4) ---

19	EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL: int = EEG_TRIAL_SHAPE[0]
20	EEG_CODE_MAX: int = EEG_VOCAB_SIZE - 1

23	THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE: int = 224
24	THINGS_PATCH_SIZE: int = 16
25	TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE: int = 16384
26	TOK_DEPTH_VOCAB_SIZE: int = 8192
27	TOK_RGB_CODE_MAX: int = TOK_RGB_VOCAB_SIZE - 1
28	TOK_DEPTH_CODE_MAX: int = TOK_DEPTH_VOCAB_SIZE - 1
29	
30	
31	def pretoken_grid_num_tokens(image_size: int, patch_size: int) -> int:
32	    """Number of patch tokens for a square pretokenized image grid."""
33	    return (image_size // patch_size) ** 2
34	
35	
36	TOK_RGB_TOKENS_PER_IMAGE: int = pretoken_grid_num_tokens(
37	    THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE, THINGS_PATCH_SIZE
38	)

41	NEURAL_SENTINEL_VALUE: int = -1
42	NEURAL_PLACEHOLDER_CODE: int = 0

45	THINGS_CENTER_CROP: tuple[int, int, int, int, int] = (

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:21.934Z
1	"""Masking wrapper that skips Dirichlet budget for absent MEG/EEG samples.
2	
3	When ``meg_mask`` or ``eeg_mask`` is 0 (sentinel placeholder on disk), force
4	token budgets for the corresponding ``tok_*`` modality to zero so 4M's
5	``sequence_token_mask`` produces no decoder logits and loss is skipped.
6	"""
7	
8	from __future__ import annotations
9	
10	import random
11	from typing import Any
12	
13	import torch
14	from fourm.data.masking import UnifiedMasking
15	from fourm.data.modality_transforms import get_transform_key
16	
17	# Maps token modality -> presence-flag key loaded from shard tars.
18	PRESENCE_FLAGS: dict[str, str] = {
19	    "tok_meg": "meg_mask",
20	    "tok_eeg": "eeg_mask",
21	}
22	
23	# Flat pretokenized sequences (MEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL / EEG_TOKENS_PER_TRIAL RVQ codes).
24	# Stock ``sequence_token_mask``
25	# injects text-tokenizer sentinel ids and breaks small-vocab ``seq_token`` embeddings.
26	_NEURAL_FLAT_TOKEN_MODS = frozenset(PRESENCE_FLAGS.keys())
27	
28	
29	def _read_presence_flag(value: Any) -> bool:
30	    """Return True when neural data is present (mask == 1)."""
31	    if value is None:
32	        return True
33	    if isinstance(value, torch.Tensor):
34	        return bool(int(value.reshape(-1)[0].item()))
35	    return bool(int(value.reshape(-1)[0]))
36	
37	
38	def extract_presence_flags(mod_dict: dict) -> dict[str, bool]:
39	    """Pop ``meg_mask`` / ``eeg_mask`` from ``mod_dict`` and return presence map."""
40	    presence: dict[str, bool] = {}
41	    for tok_mod, flag_mod in PRESENCE_FLAGS.items():
42	        if flag_mod not in mod_dict:
43	            presence[tok_mod] = True
44	            continue
45	        presence[tok_mod] = _read_presence_flag(mod_dict.pop(flag_mod))
46	    return presence
47	
48	
49	def zero_absent_budgets(
50	    modality_info: dict,
51	    input_budget: list[int],
52	    target_budget: list[int | None],
53	    presence: dict[str, bool],
54	) -> tuple[list[int], list[int | None]]:
55	    """Set input/target budgets to 0 for token modalities marked absent."""
56	    input_budget = list(input_budget)
57	    target_budget = list(target_budget)
58	    for i, mod_name in enumerate(modality_info.keys()):
59	        if mod_name in presence and not presence[mod_name]:
60	            input_budget[i] = 0
61	            if target_budget[i] is not None:
62	                target_budget[i] = 0
63	    return input_budget, target_budget
64	
65	
66	class PresenceAwareUnifiedMasking(UnifiedMasking):
67	    """``UnifiedMasking`` that respects per-sample MEG/EEG presence flags."""
68	
69	    def __call__(self, mod_dict):  # noqa: D102 — mirrors upstream signature
70	        presence = extract_presence_flags(mod_dict)
71	
72	        if self.sampling_weights is not None:
73	            dir_idx = torch.multinomial(self.sampling_weights, 1).item()
74	        else:
75	            dir_idx = random.randint(0, self.num_dirichlets - 1)
76	
77	        num_input_tokens = random.randint(*self.input_tokens_range)
78	        num_target_tokens = (
79	            random.randint(*self.target_tokens_range)
80	            if self.target_tokens_range is not None
81	            else None
82	        )
83	
84	        input_token_budget = self.input_token_budget(num_input_tokens, dir_idx)
85	
86	        if num_target_tokens is not None:
87	            target_token_budget = self.target_token_budget(
88	                input_token_budget, num_target_tokens, dir_idx
89	            )
90	        else:
91	            target_token_budget = [None] * self.num_modalities
92	
93	        input_token_budget, target_token_budget = zero_absent_budgets(
94	            self.modality_info,
95	            input_token_budget,
96	            target_token_budget,
97	            presence,
98	        )
99	
100	        masked_mod_dict = {}
101	        for (mod_name, mod_info), input_budget, target_budget in zip(
102	            self.modality_info.items(),
103	            input_token_budget,
104	            target_token_budget,
105	        ):
106	            mod_type = mod_info["type"]
107	            mod_name_load = (
108	                mod_name if mod_name in mod_dict else get_transform_key(mod_name)
109	            )
110	            if mod_type == "img":
111	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.image_mask(
112	                    mod_dict[mod_name_load],
113	                    mod_info["max_tokens"],
114	                    input_budget,
115	                    target_budget,
116	                )
117	            elif mod_type == "seq":
118	                keep_scheme = (
119	                    "random"
120	                    if ("keep" not in mod_info)
121	                    else mod_info["keep"][dir_idx]
122	                )
123	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.sequence_mask(
124	                    mod_dict[mod_name_load],
125	                    mod_info["max_tokens"],
126	                    input_budget,
127	                    target_budget,
128	                    keep_scheme,
129	                )
130	            elif mod_type == "seq_token" and mod_name in _NEURAL_FLAT_TOKEN_MODS:
131	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.image_mask(
132	                    mod_dict[mod_name_load],
133	                    mod_info["max_tokens"],
134	                    input_budget,
135	                    target_budget,
136	                )
137	            elif mod_type == "seq_token":
138	                keep_scheme = (
139	                    "random"
140	                    if ("keep" not in mod_info)
141	                    else mod_info["keep"][dir_idx]
142	                )
143	                vocab_offset = mod_info.get("vocab_offset", 0)
144	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.sequence_token_mask(
145	                    mod_dict[mod_name_load],
146	                    mod_info["max_tokens"],
147	                    input_budget,
148	                    target_budget,
149	                    keep_scheme,
150	                    vocab_offset=vocab_offset,
151	                )
152	            elif mod_type == "seq_emb":
153	                keep_scheme = (
154	                    "random"
155	                    if ("keep" not in mod_info)
156	                    else mod_info["keep"][dir_idx]
157	                )
158	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.sequence_emb_mask_span(
159	                    mod_dict[mod_name_load],
160	                    mod_info["max_tokens"],
161	                    input_budget,
162	                    target_budget,
163	                    keep_scheme,
164	                )
165	            else:
166	                raise ValueError(f"Invalid modality type: {mod_type}")
167	
168	        return masked_mod_dict
169

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:31.123Z
1	"""Image augmenter for pretokenized THINGS shards without ``crop_settings`` tars."""
2	
3	from __future__ import annotations
4	
5	import numpy as np
6	from fourm.data.image_augmenter import PreTokenizedImageAugmenter
7	
8	from neural_constants import THINGS_CENTER_CROP, THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE
9	
10	DEFAULT_CROP_SETTINGS = np.array([list(THINGS_CENTER_CROP)], dtype=np.float32)
11	
12	
13	class ThingsImageAugmenter(PreTokenizedImageAugmenter):
14	    """``PreTokenizedImageAugmenter`` that falls back to center crop when needed.
15	
16	    Stock 4M always indexes ``crop_settings[0]`` even with ``no_aug=True``.
17	    THINGS pretokenized shards may omit ``crop_settings/``; this subclass
18	    supplies a fixed THINGS_IMAGE_SIZE center crop in that case.
19	    """
20	
21	    def __call__(self, mod_dict, crop_settings):
22	        if crop_settings is None:
23	            crop_settings = DEFAULT_CROP_SETTINGS
24	
25	        if self.main_domain in mod_dict and "tok" not in self.main_domain:
26	            image = (
27	                mod_dict[self.main_domain]
28	                if self.main_domain is not None
29	                else mod_dict[list(mod_dict.keys())[0]]
30	            )
31	            orig_width, orig_height = image.size
32	            orig_size = (orig_height, orig_width)
33	        else:
34	            orig_size = None
35	
36	        rand_aug_idx = 0 if self.no_aug else np.random.randint(len(crop_settings))
37	        top, left, h, w, flip = crop_settings[rand_aug_idx]
38	        crop_coords = (top, left, h, w)
39	        return crop_coords, flip, orig_size, self.target_size, rand_aug_idx

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:33.058Z
1	"""Validate 4M main + data YAML configs against stock 4M and our neural extensions."""
2	
3	from __future__ import annotations
4	
5	import re
6	from pathlib import Path
7	from typing import Any
8	
9	import braceexpand
10	import yaml
11	
12	_REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
13	_PRESENCE_FLAGS = frozenset({"meg_mask", "eeg_mask"})
14	_TRAIN_TYPES = frozenset({"multimodal"})
15	_LOSS_TYPES = frozenset({"mod", "token"})
16	
17	
18	def _resolve(repo_root: Path, path_str: str) -> Path:
19	    p = Path(path_str)
20	    return p if p.is_absolute() else (repo_root / p).resolve()
21	
22	
23	def _modalities_in_bracket(data_path: str) -> list[str]:
24	    from fourm.data.unified_datasets import extract_modality_names
25	
26	    m = re.search(r"\[([^\]]+)\]", data_path)
27	    if not m:
28	        return []
29	    return extract_modality_names(f"{{{m.group(1)}}}")
30	
31	
32	def expand_shard_urls(data_path: str) -> list[str]:
33	    """Brace-expand a 4M ``data_path``; raises if pattern is invalid."""
34	    return list(braceexpand.braceexpand(data_path))
35	
36	
37	def _parse_alphas(value: Any, n_domains: int, label: str) -> None:
38	    if value is None:
39	        return
40	    if not isinstance(value, str):
41	        raise ValueError(f"{label} must be a string or null, got {type(value)}")
42	    parts = value.split("-")
43	    if len(parts) not in (1, n_domains):
44	        raise ValueError(
45	            f"{label} has {len(parts)} value(s) but expected 1 or {n_domains} "
46	            f"(domains hyphen-separated)"
47	        )
48	    for p in parts:
49	        float(p)
50	
51	
52	def validate_dataset_config(
53	    name: str,
54	    cfg: dict[str, Any],
55	    repo_root: Path,
56	    modality_info: dict,
57	) -> list[str]:
58	    """Return list of error strings (empty = ok)."""
59	    errors: list[str] = []
60	
61	    if cfg.get("type") not in _TRAIN_TYPES:
62	        errors.append(f"{name}: type must be 'multimodal', got {cfg.get('type')!r}")
63	
64	    data_path = cfg.get("data_path", "")
65	    if not data_path:
66	        errors.append(f"{name}: missing data_path")
67	        return errors
68	
69	    if cfg.get("use_wds", True):
70	        try:
71	            urls = expand_shard_urls(data_path)
72	        except Exception as e:
73	            errors.append(f"{name}: data_path braceexpand failed: {e}")
74	            return errors
75	
76	        if any("{" in u or "}" in u for u in urls):
77	            errors.append(
78	                f"{name}: data_path has unexpanded braces (use ranges like "
79	                f"shard_{{000..026}}.tar not shard_{{000}}.tar): {data_path}"
80	            )
81	        if not urls:
82	            errors.append(f"{name}: data_path expanded to zero shard URLs")
83	
84	    in_domains = sorted(cfg.get("in_domains", "").split("-"))
85	    out_domains = sorted(cfg.get("out_domains", "").split("-"))
86	    if not in_domains or not out_domains:
87	        errors.append(f"{name}: in_domains and out_domains are required")
88	        return errors
89	
90	    for dom in in_domains + out_domains:
91	        if dom in _PRESENCE_FLAGS:
92	            errors.append(
93	                f"{name}: {dom} is a presence flag — keep it in data_path "
94	                f"brackets only, not in_domains/out_domains"
95	            )
96	        elif dom not in modality_info:
97	            errors.append(f"{name}: unknown modality {dom!r} (not in MODALITY_INFO)")
98	
99	    bracket_mods = _modalities_in_bracket(data_path)
100	    train_domains = set(in_domains) | set(out_domains)
101	    for dom in train_domains:
102	        if dom not in bracket_mods and dom not in _PRESENCE_FLAGS:
103	            errors.append(
104	                f"{name}: {dom} in in/out_domains but not in data_path "
105	                f"bracket list {bracket_mods}"
106	            )
107	
108	    main_aug = cfg.get("main_augment_domain")
109	    if main_aug and main_aug not in modality_info:
110	        errors.append(f"{name}: main_augment_domain {main_aug!r} not in MODALITY_INFO")
111	
112	    try:
113	        _parse_alphas(cfg.get("input_alphas"), len(in_domains), f"{name}.input_alphas")
114	        _parse_alphas(cfg.get("target_alphas"), len(out_domains), f"{name}.target_alphas")
115	    except ValueError as e:
116	        errors.append(str(e))
117	
118	    alphas_cfg = cfg.get("alphas_config")
119	    if alphas_cfg:
120	        if not _resolve(repo_root, alphas_cfg).is_file():
121	            errors.append(f"{name}: alphas_config not found: {alphas_cfg}")
122	
123	    return errors
124	
125	
126	def validate_data_config(
127	    data_cfg: dict[str, Any],
128	    repo_root: Path | None = None,
129	) -> list[str]:
130	    repo_root = repo_root or _REPO_ROOT
131	    import fourm_neural_modalities  # noqa: F401 — register aliases + neural mods
132	
133	    from fourm.data.modality_info import MODALITY_INFO
134	
135	    errors: list[str] = []
136	    train = data_cfg.get("train", {})
137	    datasets = train.get("datasets", {})
138	    if not datasets:
139	        return ["train.datasets is empty"]
140	
141	    weights = train.get("weights", [1.0])
142	    if len(weights) != len(datasets):
143	        errors.append(
144	            f"train.weights length {len(weights)} != "
145	            f"number of datasets {len(datasets)}"
146	        )
147	
148	    for name, ds in datasets.items():
149	        errors.extend(validate_dataset_config(name, ds, repo_root, MODALITY_INFO))
150	
151	    return errors
152	
153	
154	def validate_main_config(
155	    main_cfg: dict[str, Any],
156	    repo_root: Path | None = None,
157	) -> list[str]:
158	    repo_root = repo_root or _REPO_ROOT
159	    errors: list[str] = []
160	
161	    from fourm.models import fm
162	
163	    model = main_cfg.get("model", "")
164	    if model not in fm.__all__:
165	        errors.append(f"unknown model {model!r}; choose from fourm.models.fm.__all__")
166	
167	    if main_cfg.get("loss_type") not in _LOSS_TYPES:
168	        errors.append(f"loss_type must be one of {_LOSS_TYPES}")
169	
170	    tok_path = main_cfg.get("text_tokenizer_path", "")
171	    if tok_path and not _resolve(repo_root, tok_path).is_file():
172	        errors.append(f"text_tokenizer_path not found: {tok_path}")
173	
174	    num_workers = main_cfg.get("num_workers", 10)
175	    if num_workers is not None and int(num_workers) < 1:
176	        errors.append("num_workers must be >= 1 (stock mixture loader divides by it)")
177	
178	    batch_size = main_cfg.get("batch_size", 0)
179	    epoch_size = main_cfg.get("epoch_size", 0)
180	    if batch_size and epoch_size:
181	        steps = int(epoch_size) // (int(batch_size) * 1)
182	        if steps < 1:
183	            errors.append(
184	                f"epoch_size ({epoch_size}) // batch_size ({batch_size}) must be >= 1"
185	            )
186	
187	    data_config = main_cfg.get("data_config", "")
188	    if not data_config:
189	        errors.append("main config missing data_config")
190	        return errors
191	
192	    data_path = _resolve(repo_root, data_config)
193	    if not data_path.is_file():
194	        errors.append(f"data_config not found: {data_config}")
195	        return errors
196	
197	    with open(data_path) as f:
198	        data_cfg = yaml.safe_load(f)
199	    errors.extend(validate_data_config(data_cfg, repo_root))
200	    return errors
201	
202	
203	def load_yaml(path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
204	    with open(path) as f:
205	        return yaml.safe_load(f)
206	
207	
208	def validate_config_file(
209	    config_path: Path | str,
210	    repo_root: Path | None = None,
211	) -> list[str]:
212	    """Validate a main yaml (has data_config) or a standalone data yaml."""
213	    repo_root = repo_root or _REPO_ROOT
214	    path = _resolve(repo_root, str(config_path))
215	    cfg = load_yaml(path)
216	    if "train" in cfg and "datasets" in cfg.get("train", {}):
217	        return validate_data_config(cfg, repo_root)
218	    return validate_main_config(cfg, repo_root)

1	# Data config for THINGS multimodal training (vision + MEG + EEG).
2	# data_path shards use braceexpand ranges, e.g. shard_{000..026}.tar → shard_000.tar … shard_026.tar
3	# (shard_{000}.tar alone is wrong — braces are not expanded and the file is missing).
4	#
5	# in_domains / out_domains (hyphen-separated):
6	#   Modalities that may appear on the encoder (input) vs decoder (target) side.
7	#   Example — predict MEG from RGB only:
8	#     in_domains: tok_rgb-tok_meg
9	#     out_domains: tok_meg
10	#   Keep meg_mask / eeg_mask out of these lists (presence flags only, not trained tokens).
11	#
12	# input_alphas / target_alphas (Dirichlet concentration, one value per in/out domain):
13	#   Control how the random input/target token budget is split across modalities each step.
14	#   Higher alpha → that modality gets a larger share of tokens more often.
15	#   Use 0.0 on an in_domain to rarely/never use it as input; 0.0 on out_domain to skip as target.
16	#   Single value "1.0" applies to all listed domains. For rgb→dense mixtures see upstream
17	#   cfgs/default/4m/alphas_mixture/ and set alphas_config instead of simple alphas.
18	#
19	# train.weights: relative sampling rate when multiple entries exist under train.datasets
20	#   (e.g. [0.8, 0.2] = 80% THINGS, 20% CC12M once cc12m is uncommented).
21

23	  datasets:
24	    things:

29	      out_domains: tok_rgb-tok_depth-tok_meg-tok_eeg

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:56:49.766Z
1	"""Modal GPU wrapper for ``train_4m.py``.
2	
3	Run from repo root::
4	
5	    modal run 4m_training/modal_train.py --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml
6	
7	Dryrun on the volume (no GPU, no training — fast config/data check)::
8	
9	    modal run 4m_training/modal_train.py --dryrun --config 4m_training/configs/4m_things_data.yaml
10	
11	Image rebuilds only when ``modal_image.py`` pip/apt deps change, not when you edit YAML or Python.
12	"""
13	
14	from __future__ import annotations
15	
16	import os
17	import subprocess
18	import sys
19	from pathlib import Path
20	
21	import importlib.util
22	import modal
23	
24	def _load_modal_image():
25	    for path in (
26	        __import__("pathlib").Path("/opt/repo/4m_training/_modal_load.py"),
27	        __import__("pathlib").Path(__file__).resolve().parent / "_modal_load.py",
28	    ):
29	        if not path.is_file():
30	            continue
31	        spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("_modal_load", path)
32	        loader = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
33	        spec.loader.exec_module(loader)
34	        return loader.load_modal_image()
35	    raise ImportError("_modal_load.py not found (expected /opt/repo/4m_training on Modal)")
36	
37	
38	_mi = _load_modal_image()
39	REPO = _mi.REPO
40	ensure_fourm = _mi.ensure_fourm
41	train_image = _mi.train_image
42	training_env = _mi.training_env
43	
44	app = modal.App("train-4m-things")
45	project_volume = modal.Volume.from_name("project")
46	PROJECT = "/project"
47	
48	
49	def _run_train(config: str, dryrun: bool, n_batches: int) -> None:
50	    ensure_fourm()
51	    cfg = config
52	    if not os.path.isabs(cfg):
53	        cfg = os.path.join(REPO, cfg)
54	
55	    cmd = [
56	        sys.executable,
57	        os.path.join(REPO, "4m_training/train_4m.py"),
58	        "dryrun" if dryrun else "train",
59	        "--config",
60	        cfg,
61	    ]
62	    if dryrun:
63	        cmd.extend(["--n-batches", str(n_batches)])
64	
65	    env = training_env()
66	    print("running:", " ".join(cmd), flush=True)
67	    subprocess.run(cmd, check=True, cwd=REPO, env=env)
68	
69	
70	@app.function(
71	    image=train_image,
72	    volumes={PROJECT: project_volume},
73	    gpu="A100",
74	    timeout=60 * 60 * 24,
75	    memory=64 * 1024,
76	)
77	def train(config: str = "4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml") -> None:
78	    _run_train(config, dryrun=False, n_batches=4)
79	
80	
81	@app.function(
82	    image=train_image,
83	    volumes={PROJECT: project_volume},
84	    timeout=60 * 30,
85	    memory=32 * 1024,
86	)
87	def dryrun(
88	    config: str = "4m_training/configs/4m_things_data.yaml",
89	    n_batches: int = 4,
90	) -> None:
91	    """CPU-only dataloader smoke test — use this before paying for GPU train."""
92	    _run_train(config, dryrun=True, n_batches=n_batches)
93	
94	
95	@app.local_entrypoint()
96	def main(
97	    config: str = "4m_training/configs/4m_things_main.yaml",
98	    dryrun: bool = False,
99	    n_batches: int = 4,
100	) -> None:
101	    if dryrun:

103	    else:

519	    def __call__(self, mod_dict):
520	        """Applies input and target masking to a dictionary of modalities
521	
522	        Args:
523	            mod_dict: Dictionary of modalities
524	
525	        Returns:
526	            Dictionary containing the masked modalities
527	        """
528	        if self.sampling_weights is not None:
529	            # Sample masking scheme according to a list of weights
530	            dir_idx = torch.multinomial(self.sampling_weights, 1).item()
531	        else:
532	            # Randomly sample masking scheme
533	            dir_idx = random.randint(0, self.num_dirichlets - 1)
534	
535	        num_input_tokens = random.randint(*self.input_tokens_range)
536	        num_target_tokens = random.randint(*self.target_tokens_range) if self.target_tokens_range is not None else None
537	
538	        input_token_budget = self.input_token_budget(num_input_tokens, dir_idx)
539	
540	        if num_target_tokens is not None:
541	            target_token_budget = self.target_token_budget(input_token_budget, num_target_tokens, dir_idx)
542	        else:
543	            target_token_budget = [None] * self.num_modalities
544	
545	        masked_mod_dict = {}
546	        for (mod_name, mod_info), input_budget, target_budget in zip(self.modality_info.items(), input_token_budget, target_token_budget):
547	            mod_type = mod_info['type']
548	            mod_name_load = mod_name if mod_name in mod_dict else get_transform_key(mod_name)
549	            if mod_type == 'img':
550	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.image_mask(mod_dict[mod_name_load], mod_info['max_tokens'], input_budget, target_budget)
551	            elif mod_type == 'seq':
552	                keep_scheme = 'random' if ('keep' not in mod_info) else mod_info['keep'][dir_idx]
553	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.sequence_mask(mod_dict[mod_name_load], mod_info['max_tokens'], input_budget, target_budget, keep_scheme)
554	            elif mod_type == 'seq_token':
555	                keep_scheme = 'random' if ('keep' not in mod_info) else mod_info['keep'][dir_idx]
556	                vocab_offset =  mod_info.get('vocab_offset', 0) # Check if any space is allocated to sentinel tokens and other special tokens
557	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.sequence_token_mask(mod_dict[mod_name_load], mod_info['max_tokens'], input_budget, target_budget, keep_scheme, vocab_offset=vocab_offset)
558	            elif mod_type == "seq_emb":
559	                keep_scheme = 'random' if ('keep' not in mod_info) else mod_info['keep'][dir_idx]
560	                masked_mod_dict[mod_name] = self.sequence_emb_mask_span(mod_dict[mod_name_load], mod_info['max_tokens'], input_budget, target_budget, keep_scheme)
561	            else:
562	                raise ValueError(f"Invalid modality type: {mod_type}")
563	
564	        return masked_mod_dict

567	class TransferMasking(object):
568	    def __init__(self,
569	                 modality_info: Dict,
570	                 text_tokenizer: Optional[Tokenizer],
571	                 input_modalities: List[str],
572	                 target_modalities: List[str]):
573	        """Performs masking for transfer on a dict of modalities (both image based and sequence based modalities),
574	        by specifying which modalities are inputs and which are targets.
575	
576	        Args:
577	            modality_info: Dict with the modalities and their corresponding information
578	            text_tokenizer: Tokenizer to use for text modalities
579	            input_modalities: List of modalities to use as input
580	            target_modalities: List of modalities to use as target
581	        """
582	        self.modality_info = modality_info
583	        self.num_modalities = len(modality_info)
584	        self.min_tokens = torch.tensor([mod['min_tokens'] for mod in modality_info.values()])
585	        self.max_tokens = torch.tensor([mod['max_tokens'] for mod in modality_info.values()])
586	        self.mod_is_img = torch.tensor([mod['type'] == 'img' for mod in modality_info.values()])
587	
588	        self.input_modalities = set(input_modalities)
589	        self.target_modalities = set(target_modalities)
590	
591	        # Tokenizer for text modalities
592	        self.text_tokenizer = text_tokenizer
593	        if self.text_tokenizer is not None:
594	            self.keep_prob_decay_factor = 0.9
595	            self.sentinel_to_id = get_sentinel_to_id_mapping(text_tokenizer)
596	            self.sentinel_ids = set(self.sentinel_to_id.values())
597	            self.pad_id = text_tokenizer.token_to_id("[PAD]")
598	            self.eos_id = text_tokenizer.token_to_id("[EOS]")

601	    def input_image(self, tensor: torch.Tensor, num_tokens: int):
602	        """Applies masking for an image given as input
603	
604	        Args:
605	            tensor: Image tensor
606	            num_tokens: Number of tokens in the tensor
607	
608	        Returns:
609	            Dictionary containing the masked image tensor, the input mask, the target mask, and the decoder attention mask
610	        """
611	
612	        # Input mask
613	        input_mask = torch.zeros(num_tokens, dtype=torch.bool)
614	        # Target mask
615	        target_mask = torch.ones(num_tokens, dtype=torch.bool)
616	        # Decoder attention mask
617	        decoder_attention_mask = torch.zeros(num_tokens, dtype=torch.int)
618	
619	        return {"tensor": tensor, "input_mask": input_mask, "target_mask": target_mask, "decoder_attention_mask": decoder_attention_mask}

⚙ Read
{
  "file_path": "/Users/Siddharth/neural-foundation-model/neural-foundation-model/external/ml-4m/fourm/data/masking.py",

Tool reply2026-05-26T22:57:41.605Z
236	    def image_mask(self, tensor: torch.Tensor, num_tokens: int, input_budget: int, target_budget: int):
237	        """Applies input and target masking to an image tensor
238	
239	        Args:
240	            tensor: Image tensor
241	            num_tokens: Number of tokens in the tensor
242	            input_budget: Token budget for the input
243	            target_budget: Token budget for the target
244	
245	        Returns:
246	            Dictionary containing the masked image tensor, the input mask, the target mask, and the decoder attention mask
247	        """
248	        noise = torch.rand(num_tokens)
249	        ids_shuffle = torch.argsort(noise, dim=0)
250	
251	        input_mask = torch.ones(num_tokens, dtype=torch.bool)
252	        input_mask[:input_budget] = 0
253	        input_mask = torch.gather(input_mask, dim=0, index=ids_shuffle)
254	
255	        if target_budget is None:
256	            target_mask = ~input_mask
257	        else:
258	            target_mask = torch.ones(num_tokens, dtype=torch.bool)
259	            target_mask[input_budget:input_budget + target_budget] = 0
260	            target_mask = torch.gather(target_mask, dim=0, index=ids_shuffle)
261	
262	        decoder_attention_mask = torch.zeros(num_tokens, dtype=torch.int)
263	        first_mask_token = torch.argmin(target_mask + torch.arange(target_mask.shape[0], device=target_mask.device) * 1e-6)
264	        decoder_attention_mask[first_mask_token] = (~target_mask).sum()  # Equiv. to target budget
265	
266	        return {"tensor": tensor, "input_mask": input_mask, "target_mask": target_mask, "decoder_attention_mask": decoder_attention_mask}
267	
268	    def sequence_token_mask(self, sequence_ids: str, max_tokens: int, input_budget: int, target_budget: int, keep_scheme: str, vocab_offset: int):
269	        """Applies input and target masking to a sequence of tokens (e.g. DINOv2 global tokens)
270	        The keep probability is sampled from a cosine schedule and does not depend on the number of tokens in the sequence.
271	        If the keep probability results in a sequence that is too long, then it is lowered until the sequence is short enough.
272	
273	        Args:
274	            sequence_ids: Sequence ids
275	            max_tokens: Maximum number of tokens in the sequence
276	            input_budget: Token budget for the input
277	            target_budget: Token budget for the target
278	            keep_scheme: Scheme for sampling the keep probability
279	            vocab_offset: Offset to avoid overlap with sentinel tokens
280	
281	        Returns:
282	            Dictionary containing the masked sequence tensor, the input mask, the target mask, and the decoder attention mask
283	        """
284	        seq_ids = sequence_ids 
285	        seq_ids = seq_ids + vocab_offset # Avoid overlap with sentinel tokens (needs to be substracted after decoding)
286	
287	        # If input budget is 0, treat it as if the whole sequence is completely masked
288	        if input_budget == 0:
289	            keep_prob = 0.
290	            input_seq_ids = []
291	            _, target_seq_ids = simple_span_masking(seq_ids, self.sentinel_to_id, keep_prob)
292	        else:
293	            if keep_scheme == 'random':
294	                keep_prob = sample_uniform(0, 1)
295	            elif keep_scheme == 'all':
296	                keep_prob = 1.0
297	            elif keep_scheme == 'binary':
298	                keep_prob = random.choice([0., 1.])
299	            else:
300	                raise ValueError(f"Invalid keep scheme for sequence masking: {keep_scheme}")
301	
302	            input_seq_ids, target_seq_ids = simple_span_masking(seq_ids, self.sentinel_to_id, keep_prob)
303	            # Keep lowering the keep_prob while we are over-budget
304	            while len(input_seq_ids) > input_budget:
305	                keep_prob = keep_prob * self.keep_prob_decay_factor
306	                input_seq_ids, target_seq_ids = simple_span_masking(seq_ids, self.sentinel_to_id, keep_prob)
307	
308	        # Span masking can add up to (max_tokens + 1) * 2 tokens for input + target
309	        max_length = (max_tokens + 1) * 2
310	        tensor = torch.ones(max_length, dtype=torch.int) * self.pad_id
311	        input_mask = torch.ones(max_length, dtype=torch.bool)
312	        target_mask = torch.ones(max_length, dtype=torch.bool)
313	        decoder_attention_mask = torch.zeros(max_length, dtype=torch.int)
314	
315	        # Set input and input mask
316	        tensor[:len(input_seq_ids)] = torch.tensor(input_seq_ids, dtype=torch.int)
317	        input_mask[:len(input_seq_ids)] = 0
318	
319	        if target_budget is None or len(target_seq_ids) <= target_budget:
320	            tensor[input_budget:input_budget + len(target_seq_ids)] = torch.tensor(target_seq_ids, dtype=torch.int)
321	            target_mask[input_budget:input_budget + len(target_seq_ids)] = 0
322	            decoder_attention_mask[input_budget:input_budget + len(target_seq_ids)] = 1
323	        else:
324	            # Randomly choose sentinel token.
325	            sentinel_indices = [i for i, token_id in enumerate(target_seq_ids) if token_id in self.sentinel_ids]
326	            # If there is more than 1 sentinel, avoid sampling the very last one which indicates the end of the sequence
327	            chosen_sentinel = np.random.randint(max(1, len(sentinel_indices) - 1))
328	            # If length starting at this token g.t. budget, truncate until budget is reached
329	            if len(target_seq_ids) - sentinel_indices[chosen_sentinel] >= target_budget:
330	                target_seq_ids = target_seq_ids[sentinel_indices[chosen_sentinel]:sentinel_indices[chosen_sentinel] + target_budget]
331	            # Otherwise, select earliest sentinel token such that we don't go over budget
332	            # Note: We could also use the randomly chosen sentinel token, but that would waste budget
333	            else:
334	                for idx in sentinel_indices:
335	                    if len(target_seq_ids) - idx <= target_budget:
336	                        target_seq_ids = target_seq_ids[idx:]
337	                        break
338	
339	            tensor[input_budget:input_budget + len(target_seq_ids)] = torch.tensor(target_seq_ids, dtype=torch.int)
340	            target_mask[input_budget:input_budget + len(target_seq_ids)] = 0
341	            decoder_attention_mask[input_budget:input_budget + len(target_seq_ids)] = 1
342	
343	        return {"tensor": tensor, "input_mask": input_mask, "target_mask": target_mask, "decoder_attention_mask": decoder_attention_mask}
344

352	            sequence: Sequence, can be either a str or list of strings
353	            max_tokens: Maximum number of tokens in the sequence
354	            input_budget: Token budget for the input
355	            target_budget: Token budget for the target

87	    def forward(self, d : Dict[str, torch.Tensor]) -> Dict[str, torch.Tensor]:
88	        """
89	        Forward pass through embedding module, transforming sequence of ids to sequence of embeddings.
90	        Creates corresponding modality and positional embeddings and adds them to the dict.
91	
92	        Args:
93	            d (Dict[str, torch.Tensor]): Modality dict with at least the following keys:
94	                - 'tensor' (torch.Tensor): Input token sequence for each batch. Shape (B, L) where B is the batch size and L is the sequence length.
95	                - 'input_mask' (torch.Tensor): Mask for valid tokens in the input sequence (set to 0 for valid tokens and 1 otherwise). Shape (B, L).
96	
97	        Returns:
98	            Dict[str, torch.Tensor]: Modality dict with added keys:
99	                - 'x' (torch.Tensor): Embedded token sequence. Shape (B, L, D) where D is the embedding dimension.
100	                - 'emb' (torch.Tensor): Sum of positional and modality embeddings for the input sequence. Shape (B, L, D).
101	        """
102	        ids = d['tensor']
103	        B = ids.shape[0]
104	        assert self.dim_tokens is not None, 'Need to call init(dim_tokens) function first'
105	
106	        # Map to embedding
107	        x = self.token_emb(ids)
108	
109	        expanded_pos_emb = repeat(self.pos_emb, "() n d -> b n d", b=B)
110	        # Input pos encoding
111	        input_mask = d['input_mask']
112	        input_pos_id = (~input_mask).int().cumsum(dim=1) - 1
113	        input_pos_id[input_mask] = 0
114	        input_pos_emb = torch.gather(expanded_pos_emb, dim=1, index=repeat(input_pos_id, "b n -> b n d", d=expanded_pos_emb.shape[2]))
115	        input_pos_emb[input_mask] = 0
116	
117	        x_emb = input_pos_emb + self.mod_emb
118	
119	        d['x'] = x
120	        d['emb'] = x_emb
121	        return d

98	    def forward_embed(self, d: Dict[str, torch.Tensor]) -> Dict[str, torch.Tensor]:
99	        """
100	        Forward pass through embedding module, transforming sequence of ids to sequence of embeddings.
101	        Creates corresponding modality and positional embeddings and adds them to the dict.
102	
103	        Args:
104	            d (Dict[str, torch.Tensor]): Modality dict, with at least the following keys:
105	                - 'tensor' (torch.Tensor): Token sequence for each batch. Shape (B, L) where B is the batch size and L is the sequence length.
106	                - 'target_mask' (torch.Tensor): Mask for valid tokens in the target sequence (set to 0 for valid tokens and 1 otherwise). Shape (B, L).
107	
108	        Returns:
109	            Dict[str, torch.Tensor]: Modality dict with added keys:
110	                - 'x' (torch.Tensor): Embedded token sequence. Shape (B, L, D) where D is the embedding dimension.
111	                - 'emb' (torch.Tensor): Sum of positional and modality embeddings for the target sequence. Shape (B, L, D).
112	                - 'ids' (torch.Tensor): Original token sequence from input dict. Shape (B, L).
113	        """
114	        ids = d['tensor']
115	        B = ids.shape[0]
116	        assert self.dim_tokens is not None, 'Need to call init(dim_tokens) function first'
117	
118	        # Map to embedding
119	        x = self.token_emb(ids)
120	
121	        expanded_pos_emb = repeat(self.pos_emb, "() n d -> b n d", b=B)
122	
123	        # Target pos encoding
124	        target_mask = d['target_mask']
125	        target_pos_id = (~target_mask).int().cumsum(dim=1) - 1
126	        target_pos_id[target_mask] = 0
127	        # Sometimes target sequence is over max length, it will be truncated in decoder
128	        target_pos_id[target_pos_id >= self.max_length] = 0
129	        target_pos_emb = torch.gather(expanded_pos_emb, dim=1, index=repeat(target_pos_id, "b n -> b n d", d=expanded_pos_emb.shape[2]))
130	        target_pos_emb[target_mask] = 0
131	
132	        x_emb = target_pos_emb + self.mod_emb
133	
134	
135	        d['x'] = x
136	        d['emb'] = x_emb
137	        d['ids'] = d['tensor']
138	
139	        return d
140	
141	    def forward_logits(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
142	        """
143	        Forward pass through output projection layer, transforming sequence of embeddings to logits.
144	
145	        Args:
146	            x (torch.Tensor): Output tokens from the decoder. Shape (B, M, D)
147	        
148	        Returns:
149	            torch.Tensor: Logits for each token in the sequence. Shape (B, M, V)
150	        """
151	        logits = self.to_logits(x)
152	        return logits
